# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="4ef11-104">.NET Framework에서 사용되지 않는 형식</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4ef11-104">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>

<a name="introduction"></a> <span data-ttu-id="4ef11-105">이 문서의 표에는 .NET Framework 4.5 및 .NET Framework 4.6에서 사용되지 않은 형식이 어셈블리별로 나열되어 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4ef11-105">The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the .NET Framework 4.5 and the .NET Framework 4.6, organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4ef11-106">사용하지 않는 형식과 각 어셈블리에서 권장되는 대체 형식의 목록을 보려면 다음 링크를 사용합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4ef11-106">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4ef11-107">이러한 형식은 사용되지 않으므로 해당 형식의 멤버도 모두 사용되지 않습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4ef11-107">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4ef11-108">.NET Framework 클래스 라이브러리의 사용되지 않는 멤버에 대한 추가 목록은 [사용되지 않는 멤버](obsolete-members.md)를 참조하십시오.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4ef11-108">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](obsolete-members.md).</span></span>

<a name="obsolete_types_in_system_assemblies"></a>

## <a name="obsolete-types-in-system-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="4ef11-135">시스템 어셈블리에서 사용되지 않는 형식</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4ef11-135">Obsolete Types in System Assemblies</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4ef11-136">다음 표에서는 시스템 어셈블리에서 사용되지 않는 것으로 선언된 형식을 보여 줍니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4ef11-136">The following tables list the types that have been declared obsolete in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4ef11-137">이러한 어셈블리는 .NET Framework를 대상으로 하는 일반\-용도의 애플리케이션 개발에 사용됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4ef11-137">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>

<a name="obsolete_types_in_microsoft_assemblies"></a>

## <a name="obsolete-types-in-microsoft-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="4ef11-926">Microsoft 어셈블리에서 사용되지 않는 형식</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4ef11-926">Obsolete Types in Microsoft Assemblies</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4ef11-927">다음 단원에서는 Microsoft 어셈블리에서 사용되지 않는 형식을 보여 줍니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4ef11-927">The following sections list the obsolete types in Microsoft assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4ef11-928">이러한 어셈블리는 Microsoft.JScript.dll, Microsoft.VisualC.dll 등의 개별 언어를 대상으로 하는 어셈블리와 같은 특수 용도의 어셈블리입니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4ef11-928">These assemblies are special-purpose assemblies such as assemblies that target an individual language (for example, Microsoft.JScript.dll or Microsoft.VisualC.dll).</span></span>

<a name="IEHost"></a>

### <a name="assembly-iehostdll-and-ieexecexe"></a><span data-ttu-id="4ef11-929">어셈블리: IEHost.dll 및 IEExec.exe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4ef11-929">Assembly: IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4ef11-930">IEHost.dll 및 IEExec.exe 어셈블리는 .NET Framework에서 제거되었습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4ef11-930">The IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe assemblies have been removed from the .NET Framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4ef11-931">해당 형식 및 멤버는 모두 사용되지 않으며 .NET Framework 4부터 지원되지 않습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4ef11-931">All of their types and their members are obsolete and are not supported as of the .NET Framework 4.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4ef11-932">이러한 어셈블리는 Windows Forms 컨트롤을 호스팅하여 Internet Explorer에서 실행 파일을 실행하기 위해 사용되었습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4ef11-932">These assemblies were used to host Windows Forms controls and to run executables in Internet Explorer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4ef11-933">ClickOnce, XBAP(XAML 브라우저 애플리케이션) 및 Microsoft Silverlight를 대신 사용하는 것이 좋습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4ef11-933">Recommended alternatives include ClickOnce, XAML browser applications (XBAP), and Microsoft Silverlight.</span></span>
